<p><strong><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt; color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Baba Times Digest | 24 February 2015 15.39 EST | New York Edition</span></span></span><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><br style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;" /></span></span></strong></p>

<![endif]--> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>Isavasya Upanishad<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>Divine Life Society Publication: </b><span style="color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://www.swami-krishnananda.org/disc/disc_186.html"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><b>Commentary on the Isavasya Upanishad</b></span></a></span><b> by Sri Swami Krishnananda<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Verses</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">m pram ada, pram idam, prt pram udacyate |<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">prasya pram dya pram evvaiyate ||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">That is Full; this is full. From the Full does the Full proceed. </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">After the coming of the Full from the full, the Full alone remains.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Om vsyam ida sarvam yat ki ca jagaty jagat | <o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">tena tyaktena bhujitha, ma gdha kasyasvid dhanam ||1||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">OM. All this  whatsoever moves on the earth  should be covered by the Lord. Protect (your Self) through that detachment. Do not covet anybodys wealth. (or  Do not covet, for whose is wealth?)</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">kurvann eveha karmi jijviet ata sam | </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">eva tvayi nnyathetosti na karma lipyate nare ||2||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">By doing karma indeed should one wish to live here for a hundred years. For a man such as you (who wants to live thus), there is no other way than this, whereby karma may not cling to you.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">asury nma te lok andhena tamas vt | </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">ts te pretybhigacchanti ye ke ctmahano jan ||3||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Those worlds of devils are covered by blinded darkness. Those people that kill the Self go to them after giving up this body.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">anejad eka manaso javyo nainad dev pnuvan prvamarat | </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">tad dhvatonyn-atyeti tihat tasminn apo mtariv dadhti ||4||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">It is unmoving, one, and faster than the mind. The senses could not overtake It, since It ran ahead. Remaining stationary, It outruns all other runners. It being there, Matarisva allots (or supports) all activities.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">tad ejati tan naijati tad dre tad vad antike | </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">tad antarasya sarvasya tad u sarvasysya bhyata ||5||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">That moves, That does not move; That is far off, That is very near; That is inside all, and That is outside all.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">yas tu sarvi bhtani tmany evnupayati |</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">sarvabhteu catmna tato na vijugupsate ||6||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">He who sees all beings in the very Self, and the Self in all beings, feels no hatred by that (realisation).</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">yasmin sarvi bhtny tmaivbhd vijnata | <o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">tatra ko moha ka oka ekatvam anupayata ||7||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">When to the man of realisation all beings become the very Self, then what delusion and what sorrow can there be for that seer of oneness?</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">sa paryagc chukram, akyam, avraam, asnviram, uddham, appaviddham |</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">kavir man, paribh, svayambh, ythtathyatorthn vyadadhc chvatbhyas sambhya ||8||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">He is all-pervasive, pure, bodyless, without wound, without sinews, taintless, untouched by sin, omniscient, ruler of mind, transcendent, and self-existent; he has duly allotted the (respective) duties to the eternal years (i.e., to the eternal creators called by that name).</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">andha tama pravianti yovidym upasate | </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">tato bhya iva te tamo ya u vidyy rat ||9||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Those who worship <em><span style="font-style: normal;">avidya</span></em>, enter into blinded darkness; but into greater darkness than that, enter they who are engaged in <em><span style="font-style: normal;">vidya</span></em>.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">anyad evhur vidyay anyad hur avidyay | </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">iti uruma dhrm ye nas tad vicacakire ||10||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">They say that by <em><span style="font-style: normal;">vidya</span></em> a really different result is achieved, and by <em><span style="font-style: normal;">avidya</span></em> a different result. Thus have we heard (the teaching of) those wise men who explained that to us.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">vidy cvidy ca yas tad vedobhayam saha | </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">avidyay mtyu trtv vidyaymtam anute ||11||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">He who knows these two  <em><span style="font-style: normal;">vidya</span></em> and <em><span style="font-style: normal;">avidya</span></em>  together, attains immortality through <em><span style="font-style: normal;">vidya</span></em>, by crossing over death through <em><span style="font-style: normal;">avidya</span></em>.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">andha tama pravianti yesambhtim upsate |<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">tato bhuya iva te tamo ya u sambhuty rat ||12||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Those who worship the Unmanifested, enter into blinding darkness; but those who are devoted to the Manifest, enter into greater darkness.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">anyad evah sambhavd anyad hur asambhavt | </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">iti uruma dhrm ye nas tad vicacakire ||13||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">They spoke of different results from the worship of the Manifested, and they spoke of different results from the worship of the Unmanifested  thus we have heard (the teaching of those wise men.)</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">sambhti ca vina ca yas tad vedobhaya saha | </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">vinena mtyu trtv sambhty amtam anute ||14||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">He who knows these two  the Unmanifested and Destruction  together, attains immortality through the Unmanifested by crossing death through Destruction.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">hiramayena ptrea satyasypihitam mukham |</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">tat tva pan pvu satyadharmya daye ||15||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">The face of the Truth (Brahman in the solar orb) is concealed with a golden vessel. Do thou, O Sun, open it so as to be seen by me, who am by nature truthful (or, who am the performer of rightful duties).</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">pann ekare yama srya prjpatya vyha ramn samha teja | </span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">yat te rpa kalyatama tat te paymi yo sv asau purua, soham asmi ||16||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">O Thou, who art the nourisher, the solitary traveller, the controller, the acquirer, the son of Prajapati, do remove Thy rays, do gather up thy dazzle. I shall behold that form of Thine, which is the most benign. I am that very person that is yonder (in the sun).</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">vyur anilam amtam athedam bhasmnta arram | <o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">aum krato smara kta smara krato smara kta smara ||17||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Let my vital force now attain the (all-pervading) immortal air; and now let this body be reduced to ashes. OM, O my mind remember  remember all that has been done. Remember  remember all that has been done.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">agne naya supath rye asmn vivni deva vayunni vidvn |</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> yuyodhyasmaj juharam eno bhyih te nama-uktim vidhema ||18||</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">O Fire! O God! Knowing as Thou doest all our deeds, lead us by the good path for the enjoyment of the fruits of our deeds; remove us from all crooked sins. We offer Thee many words of Salutation!</span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span class="bodytahoma" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">m ntih ntih ntih!</span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> <a name="_GoBack">Om. May there be peace, peace, peace!</a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
